[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.poi.POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mPOIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:74[0m[1m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         DEDUP_TOKEN: ac6e69a60acc10da                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer-based fuzz test on Apache POI’s POIFSDump utility triggered a              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception due to a file path traversal. The           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitization logic in `FilePathTraversal` detected user-controlled `..` segments    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that escape the intended output directory, flagging a critical security issue. The  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         error surfaces when the fuzzer drives `POIFSDump.dump`, which writes to a path      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         constructed from parsed POIFS entries.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Type                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The fuzzer report indicates a **File Path Traversal** vulnerability, as enforced  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         by the `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal` checks.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - What Happened                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. The fuzz harness [1m([0m`POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m feeds arbitrary     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         POIFS data into `POIFSDump.main`.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. During execution, `POIFSDump.dump` attempts to write entry data under a        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory structure named after POIFS entries.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. An entry named “Root Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m” causes the path       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         construction logic to resolve to `[35m/tmp/.../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`, escaping the intended [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sandbox directory.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. `FilePathTraversal.check` and `checkPath` detect the traversal pattern and     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         raise `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`, stopping execution.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Key Observations and Findings                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The path traversal originates in the logic that maps POIFS entry names directly [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to filesystem paths without sufficient normalization or sanitization.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The Jazzer sanitizer hooks into all file-writing APIs used by POIFSDump,        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         indicating comprehensive coverage of file operations.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The harness merely exercises POIFSDump; it does not introduce the traversal     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         itself. The unsafe behavior lies in how entry names are handled at runtime.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Review                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. **org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump** – how it constructs output paths   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         from entry names and opens files.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. **FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook** – the sanitizer hook showing which APIs [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         are guarded and how.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Any auxiliary methods used for normalizing or sanitizing entry names before    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         filesystem use.                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The broader POIFS parsing and entry-naming conventions to understand if other  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         APIs share the same pattern.                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A holistic review of path construction in POIFSDump [1m([0mand related POI utilities[1m)[0m is  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         recommended to identify all code paths where user-supplied names might lead to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory escapes.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== Java Exception: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFile path traversal: [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/expander-tmp2427935457273969321/output/q/r/s/t/input.bin_dump/[0m[95mRoot[0m[39m [0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:    public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry root, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfor[0m[1;39m([0m[39mIterator<Entry> it = [0m[1;35mroot.getEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;35mit.hasNext[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:            Entry entry = [0m[1;35mit.next[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry instanceof DocumentNode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:                final DocumentNode node = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDocumentNode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m entry;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:                final byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDocumentInputStream is = new [0m[1;35mDocumentInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:                   bytes = [0m[1;35mIOUtils.toByteArray[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream out = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mout.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m111[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry instanceof DirectoryEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m112[0m[39m:                DirectoryEntry dir = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mentry;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:                File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m114[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mfile.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mfile.mkdirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Could not create directory "[0m[39m + [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir, file[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `POIFSDump.dump` methods construct filesystem paths by directly passing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw POIFS entry names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `[0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` constructor.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malicious or fuzzed entry names containing path separators [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`, `\`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lead to directory escapes, triggering Jazzer’s [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to reflect the POIFS directory hierarchy in the output dump.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter any of the fuzzer harness, test code, or utility methods [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside of `POIFSDump`.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We should keep existing exception behavior if directories or files cannot be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreated.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Sanitization Strategy[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a private helper method in `POIFSDump` to sanitize entry names:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Trim leading/trailing whitespace.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Normalize to the final path segment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdropping any embedded separators or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: use `[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrimmedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Guard against resulting names of `[0m[32m"."[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m".."[0m[39m`, or empty strings by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprefixing an underscore.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invoke this sanitizer on every user-controlled name before constructing `File`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobjects.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump`, add:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.nio.file.Path;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import java.nio.file.Paths;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Define within the class [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., just after the class declaration[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * Sanitizes a POIFS entry name so it cannot escape the intended dump [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * Drops any path components, strips traversal segments, and ensures [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-empty valid names.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static String [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString rawName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          String trimmed = [0m[1;35mrawName.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Keep only the final segment, removing any embedded [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseparators/traversal[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path p = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrimmed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          String baseName = [0m[1;35mp.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Prevent [0m[32m"."[0m[39m or [0m[32m".."[0m[39m or empty names[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mbaseName.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m".."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              baseName = [0m[32m"_"[0m[39m + baseName;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return baseName;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Update the dump routines:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry root, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        * Replace:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          with[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        * Replace:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          with[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `public static void main` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere `[0m[1;35mroot.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is used to seed the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfirst directory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        * Replace:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdumpDir, [0m[1;35mroot.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          with[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdumpDir, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mroot.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By collapsing any multi-segment names to their last component, we neutralize [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`..[0m[35m/[0m[39m` or absolute paths.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach preserves the intended dump structure while eliminating [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory traversal risks.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since all usages of entry names are channelled through the sanitizer, we block[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious fuzz inputs without touching harness or external libraries.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid POIFS entry names that legitimately include slashes [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflattened, but POIFS specs generally restrict entry names to simple tokens.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential filename collisions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo entries sanitizing to the same base name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain a theoretical risk but mirror the existing risk of same-named entries; [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddressing that would require a more stateful mapping—out of scope for this patch.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests for `POIFSDump` should continue to pass, as they use standard [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry names.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Further Iteration Needed[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer fully addresses the path-traversal vector identified by Jazzer.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external dependencies are modified, and fuzzing harness remains untouched, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msatisfying all constraints.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m[12/27/25 19:40:22][0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.ANALYZE                  ]8;id=438259;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=173299;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mn evals: [1;36m2[0m, patch status: PatchStatus.UNCOMPILABLE[1m)[0m                                 [2m               [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                      [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1m([0m[1;35mfile.toPath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.getParent[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  [1m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Patch [33mResult[0m===                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===[33mIssue[0m===                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         == Java Exception: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical:    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         File path traversal:                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/expander-tmp2427935457273969321/output/q/r/s/t/input.bin_dump/[0m[95mRoot[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0mFilePathTraversal.j [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         av[1;92ma:346[0m[1m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.checkPath[0m[1m([0mFilePathTravers [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         al.jav[1;92ma:293[0m[1m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook[0m[1m([0mFilePath [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Traversal.jav[1;92ma:177[0m[1m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at [1;35morg.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSDump.jav[1;92ma:108[0m[1m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at [1;35morg.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.main[0m[1m([0mPOIFSDump.jav[1;92ma:80[0m[1m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.poi.POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mPOIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:74[0m[1m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         DEDUP_TOKEN: ac6e69a60acc10da                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The fuzzer run on `POIFSDump` reported a critical Jazzer security issue: a file     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path traversal when dumping POIFS entries. In response, a patch was proposed to     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         introduce a `sanitizeEntryName` helper in `POIFSDump.java` that strips path         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         components and traversal segments from entry names before creating files or         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directories. After applying the patch, the Java compilation of `POIFSDump.java`     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         failed with six “class, interface, or enum expected” errors, indicating that the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         new method was inserted outside the body of any class or interface.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The Jazzer fuzzer triggered a                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Stack trace points to `FilePathTraversal.check` in the sanitizer tooling,      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         propagating through `POIFSDump.dump` and `POIFSDump.main` into                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The sanitizer flagged an input that contained `..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         demonstrating that untrusted entry names from a POIFS stream can escape the         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intended dump directory.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability arises because `POIFSDump` uses raw entry names [1m([0mvia         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m as file or directory names without any normalization or          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         filtering.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Both document entries and nested directory entries invoke constructors like    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent, [1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m`, triggering the sanitizer’s              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path-first-argument hook.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - No existing sanitization or validation logic prevents traversal components     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`..`[1m)[0m from being used in entry names.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Imports added:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```java                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              import java.nio.file.Path;                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - New helper inserted:                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```java                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [35m/[0m**                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               * Sanitizes a POIFS entry name so it cannot escape the intended dump          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               * Drops any path components, strips traversal segments, and ensures non-empty [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         valid names.                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               *[35m/[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              private static String [1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1m([0mString rawName[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  String trimmed = [1;35mrawName.trim[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  Path p = [1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0mtrimmed[1m)[0m;                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  String baseName = [1;35mp.getFileName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  if [1m([0m[1;35mbaseName.isEmpty[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m || [32m"."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1m([0mbaseName[1m)[0m || [32m".."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1m([0mbaseName[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                      baseName = [32m"_"[0m + baseName;                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  [1m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  return baseName;                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [1m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Calls to `new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent, [1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m` and similar were replaced with    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1m([0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m` in three locations: root directory creation,   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         document output, and nested directory creation.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - After applying these changes, the Gradle build log showed six compilation      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         errors at the location of `private static String [1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, all       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         complaining “class, interface, or enum expected.” This indicates the method was     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         placed outside the scope of the surrounding class.                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Post-Patch Log Excerpt                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            ```                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            [35m/src/poi/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/poifs/dev/[0m[95mPOIFSDump.java[0m:[1;36m41[0m: error: class, [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         interface, or enum expected                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                private static String [1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1m([0mString rawName[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                               ^                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            [1m[[0msimilar errors for following lines[1m][0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            ```                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The build stops at `:poi:compileJava` with the above errors, preventing any    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         further progress.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Verify the location and surrounding braces in `POIFSDump.java` to ensure the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         new method is declared inside the `public class POIFSDump [1m{[0m [33m...[0m [1m}[0m` block.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Confirm matching class-level opening and closing braces so that the helper     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         method does not fall outside the class.                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Review all code paths in `POIFSDump` [1m([0mincluding `dump`, `main`, and any        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         utility methods[1m)[0m that construct `File` objects from entry names to ensure           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         consistent use of the sanitizer.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Examine other POI utilities or examples that use raw file names in similar     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         contexts for potential path traversal gaps.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Correct the placement of the `sanitizeEntryName` helper and necessary import so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the code compiles:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Remove the current helper method and the `import java.nio.file.Path;` that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwere inadvertently inserted outside the class body.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Inside `POIFSDump.java`, add the import at the top alongside existing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimports:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        import java.nio.file.Path;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Locate the class declaration:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        public final class POIFSDump [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     and immediately after the private constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`private [0m[1;35mPOIFSDump[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsert the `sanitizeEntryName` helper method. This ensures it lives within the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass’s braces and resolves the “class, interface, or enum expected” errors.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Harden every file or directory creation site in `POIFSDump` to use sanitized [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry names:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `[0m[1;35mmain[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m args[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, replace[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdumpDir, [0m[1;35mroot.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdumpDir, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mroot.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the `public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry root, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Change the document-output path:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Change the nested-directory path:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. In the overload `public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOIFSFileSystem fs, int startBlock, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mString name, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, name[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      should become[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      even though `name` values are constants, this keeps the approach uniform and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture-proof.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation steps:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Open `poi/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/poifs/dev/POIFSDump.java`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – At the imports section [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., after `import java.nio.file.Files; import [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjava.nio.file.Paths;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m add:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         import java.nio.file.Path;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Scroll to just after the private constructor and insert:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * Sanitizes a POIFS entry name so it cannot escape the intended dump [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * Drops any path components, strips traversal segments, and ensures [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-empty valid names.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static String [0m[1;35msanitizeEntryName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString rawName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             String trimmed = [0m[1;35mrawName.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Convert to Path to strip any parent components[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             Path p = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrimmed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             String baseName = [0m[1;35mp.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Guard against empty or purely traversal names[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mbaseName.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m".."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 baseName = [0m[32m"_"[0m[39m + baseName;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return baseName;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Locate and update the file-and-directory creation sites as described in step [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m.[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Ensure matching braces remain intact.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Placing `sanitizeEntryName` inside the class body fixes the compilation errors[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m“class, interface, or enum expected”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Uniformly replacing raw entry names with the sanitized result prevents path [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal by stripping “..” segments and embedded directories.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Importing `java.nio.file.Path` alongside existing `Files` and `Paths` imports [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlets the helper compile without touching external dependencies.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – This approach preserves all existing dumping logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstructure, recursion, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperty/mini-stream dumping[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and requires no changes to the fuzzer harness, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal libraries, or test code.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Potential side effects: benign nested names with slashes or dots are flattened[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto their base name, which is acceptable for a dump utility. No existing [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality is dropped.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verification:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Rebuild the `poi` module [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`.[0m[35m/[0m[95mgradlew[0m[39m :poi:compileJava`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and ensure no “class, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterface, or enum expected” errors.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Run existing POIFSDump examples to confirm that dump outputs still occur and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat traversal attempts [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., entry names containing “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are neutralized by the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhelper.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Rerun the Jazzer fuzzer on `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer` to verify the [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer no longer triggers.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
